  25 /**

  36      * @see <a
  37      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se7/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.1-200-A">
  38      * The ClassFile Structure in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
  39      */
  40     public static final int JVM_CLASSFILE_MAGIC = 0xCAFEBABE;

 212     /**
 213      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 214      *
 215      * @see <a
 216      * href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.5'>
 217      * Flag definitions for Fields in the Java Virtual Machine Specification
 218      * (Java SE 8 Edition).</a>
 219      * @see <a
 220      * href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.6'>
 221      * Flag definitions for Methods in the Java Virtual Machine Specification
 222      * (Java SE 8 Edition).</a>
 223      * @see <a
 224      * href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.7.6-300-D.1-D.1'>
 225      * Flag definitions for Classes in the Java Virtual Machine Specification
 226      * (Java SE 8 Edition).</a>
 227      */
 228     public static final short ACC_PUBLIC = 0x0001;
 229 
 230     /**
 231      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 232      *
 233      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 234      */
 235     public static final short ACC_PRIVATE = 0x0002;
 236 
 237     /**
 238      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 239      *
 240      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 241      */
 242     public static final short ACC_PROTECTED = 0x0004;
 243 
 244     /**
 245      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 246      *
 247      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 248      */
 249     public static final short ACC_STATIC = 0x0008;
 250 
 251     /**
 252      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 253      *
 254      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 255      */
 256     public static final short ACC_FINAL = 0x0010;
 257

 259      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 260      *
 261      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 262      */
 263     public static final short ACC_SYNCHRONIZED = 0x0020;
 264

 266      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 267      *
 268      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 269      */
 270     public static final short ACC_VOLATILE = 0x0040;
 271

 274      *

 276      */
 277     public static final short ACC_BRIDGE = 0x0040;

 284     public static final short ACC_TRANSIENT = 0x0080;

 291     public static final short ACC_VARARGS = 0x0080;

 340     public static final short ACC_ENUM = 0x4000;

 343      * One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.

 345      * @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 347     public static final short ACC_MANDATED = (short) 0x8000;

 364     /**
 365      * The names of the access flags.
 366      */
 367     private static final String[] ACCESS_NAMES = {
 368         "public", "private", "protected", "static", "final", "synchronized",
 369         "volatile", "transient", "native", "interface", "abstract", "strictfp",
 370         "synthetic", "annotation", "enum"
 371     };
 372 
 373     /**
 374      * @since 6.0
 375      */
 376     public static final int ACCESS_NAMES_LENGTH = ACCESS_NAMES.length;
 377 
 378     /**
 379      * @param index
 380      * @return the ACCESS_NAMES entry at the given index
 381      * @since 6.0
 382      */
 383     public static String getAccessName(final int index) {
 384         return ACCESS_NAMES[index];
 385     }

 387     /*
 388      * The description of the constant pool is at:
 389      * http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4
 390      * References below are to the individual sections
 391      */
 392     /**
 393      * Marks a constant pool entry as type UTF-8.
 394      *
 395      * @see <a
 396      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.7">
 397      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 398      */
 399     public static final byte CONSTANT_Utf8 = 1;
 400 
 401     /**
 402      * Marks a constant pool entry as type Integer.
 403      *
 404      * @see <a
 405      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.4">
 406      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 407      */
 408     public static final byte CONSTANT_Integer = 3;
 409 
 410     /**
 411      * Marks a constant pool entry as type Float.
 412      *
 413      * @see <a
 414      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.4">
 415      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 416      */
 417     public static final byte CONSTANT_Float = 4;
 418 
 419     /**
 420      * Marks a constant pool entry as type Long.
 421      *
 422      * @see <a
 423      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.5">
 424      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 425      */
 426     public static final byte CONSTANT_Long = 5;
 427 
 428     /**
 429      * Marks a constant pool entry as type Double.
 430      *
 431      * @see <a
 432      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.5">
 433      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 434      */
 435     public static final byte CONSTANT_Double = 6;
 436 
 437     /**
 438      * Marks a constant pool entry as a Class
 439      *
 440      * @see <a
 441      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.1">

 443      */
 444     public static final byte CONSTANT_Class = 7;
 445 
 446     /**
 447      * Marks a constant pool entry as a Field Reference.
 448      *
 449      * @see <a
 450      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.2">

 452      */
 453     public static final byte CONSTANT_Fieldref = 9;

 455     /**
 456      * Marks a constant pool entry as type String
 457      *
 458      * @see <a
 459      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.3">
 460      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 461      */
 462     public static final byte CONSTANT_String = 8;
 463 
 464     /**
 465      * Marks a constant pool entry as a Method Reference.
 466      *
 467      * @see <a
 468      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.2">

 471     public static final byte CONSTANT_Methodref = 10;

 473     /**
 474      * Marks a constant pool entry as an Interface Method Reference.

 476      * @see <a
 477      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.2">

 479      */
 480     public static final byte CONSTANT_InterfaceMethodref = 11;
 481 
 482     /**
 483      * Marks a constant pool entry as a name and type.
 484      *
 485      * @see <a
 486      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.6">
 487      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 488      */
 489     public static final byte CONSTANT_NameAndType = 12;

 491     /**
 492      * Marks a constant pool entry as a Method Handle.

 497      */
 498     public static final byte CONSTANT_MethodHandle = 15;

 500     /**

 503      * @see <a
 504      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.9">

 507     public static final byte CONSTANT_MethodType = 16;

 509     /**
 510      * Marks a constant pool entry as an Invoke Dynamic
 511      *
 512      * @see <a
 513      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.4.10">
 514      * The Constant Pool in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 515      */
 516     public static final byte CONSTANT_InvokeDynamic = 18;
 517 
 518     /**
 519      * The names of the types of entries in a constant pool. Use getConstantName
 520      * instead
 521      */
 522     private static final String[] CONSTANT_NAMES = {
 523         "", "CONSTANT_Utf8", "", "CONSTANT_Integer",
 524         "CONSTANT_Float", "CONSTANT_Long", "CONSTANT_Double",
 525         "CONSTANT_Class", "CONSTANT_String", "CONSTANT_Fieldref",
 526         "CONSTANT_Methodref", "CONSTANT_InterfaceMethodref",
 527         "CONSTANT_NameAndType", "", "", "CONSTANT_MethodHandle",
 528         "CONSTANT_MethodType", "", "CONSTANT_InvokeDynamic"};
 529 
 530     /**
 531      *
 532      * @param index
 533      * @return the CONSTANT_NAMES entry at the given index
 534      * @since 6.0
 535      */
 536     public static String getConstantName(final int index) {
 537         return CONSTANT_NAMES[index];
 538     }

 540     /**
 541      * The name of the static initializer, also called &quot;class
 542      * initialization method&quot; or &quot;interface initialization
 543      * method&quot;. This is &quot;&lt;clinit&gt;&quot;.
 544      */
 545     public static final String STATIC_INITIALIZER_NAME = "<clinit>";
 546 
 547     /**
 548      * The name of every constructor method in a class, also called
 549      * &quot;instance initialization method&quot;. This is
 550      * &quot;&lt;init&gt;&quot;.
 551      */
 552     public static final String CONSTRUCTOR_NAME = "<init>";
 553 
 554     /**
 555      * The names of the interfaces implemented by arrays
 556      */
 557     private static final String[] INTERFACES_IMPLEMENTED_BY_ARRAYS = {"java.lang.Cloneable", "java.io.Serializable"};
 558 
 559     /**
 560      * @since 6.0
 561      */
 562     public static Iterable<String> getInterfacesImplementedByArrays() {
 563         return Collections.unmodifiableList(Arrays.asList(INTERFACES_IMPLEMENTED_BY_ARRAYS));
 564     }
 565 
 566     /**
 567      * Maximum Constant Pool entries. One of the limitations of the Java Virtual
 568      * Machine.
 569      *
 570      * @see <a
 571      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.11-100-A">
 572      * The Java Virtual Machine Specification, Java SE 8 Edition, page 330,
 573      * chapter 4.11.</a>
 574      */
 575     public static final int MAX_CP_ENTRIES = 65535;
 576 
 577     /**
 578      * Maximum code size (plus one; the code size must be LESS than this) One of
 579      * the limitations of the Java Virtual Machine. Note vmspec2 page 152
 580      * ("Limitations") says: "The amount of code per non-native, non-abstract
 581      * method is limited to 65536 bytes by the sizes of the indices in the
 582      * exception_table of the Code attribute (4.7.3), in the LineNumberTable
 583      * attribute (4.7.8), and in the LocalVariableTable attribute (4.7.9)."
 584      * However this should be taken as an upper limit rather than the defined
 585      * maximum. On page 134 (4.8.1 Static Constants) of the same spec, it says:
 586      * "The value of the code_length item must be less than 65536." The entry in
 587      * the Limitations section has been removed from later versions of the spec;
 588      * it is not present in the Java SE 8 edition.
 589      *
 590      * @see <a
 591      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.7.3-300-E">
 592      * The Java Virtual Machine Specification, Java SE 8 Edition, page 104,
 593      * chapter 4.7.</a>
 594      */
 595     public static final int MAX_CODE_SIZE = 65536; //bytes
 596 
 597     /**
 598      * The maximum number of dimensions in an array ({@value}). One of the
 599      * limitations of the Java Virtual Machine.
 600      *
 601      * @see <a
 602      * href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.3.2-150">
 603      * Field Descriptors in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 604      */
 605     public static final int MAX_ARRAY_DIMENSIONS = 255;
 606

 613      */
 614     public static final short NOP = 0;

 661     /**

 202    *  */
 203   public static final short MINOR     = MINOR_1_1;

 205   /** Maximum value for an unsigned short.
 206    */
 207   public static final int MAX_SHORT = 65535; // 2^16 - 1

 209   /** Maximum value for an unsigned byte.
 210    */
 211   public static final int MAX_BYTE  = 255; // 2^8 - 1

 213   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 214    *  @see <a href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se9/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.1-200-E.1'>
 215    *  Flag definitions for Classes in the Java Virtual Machine Specification (Java SE 9 Edition).</a>
 216    *  @see <a href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se9/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.5'>
 217    *  Flag definitions for Fields in the Java Virtual Machine Specification (Java SE 9 Edition).</a>
 218    *  @see <a href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se9/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.6'>
 219    *  Flag definitions for Methods in the Java Virtual Machine Specification (Java SE 9 Edition).</a>
 220    *  @see <a href='http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se9/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.7.6-300-D.1-D.1'>
 221    *  Flag definitions for Inner Classes in the Java Virtual Machine Specification (Java SE 9 Edition).</a>
 222    */
 223   public static final short ACC_PUBLIC       = 0x0001;
 224 
 225   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 226    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 227    */
 228   public static final short ACC_PRIVATE      = 0x0002;
 229 
 230   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 231    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 232    */
 233   public static final short ACC_PROTECTED    = 0x0004;
 234 
 235   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 236    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 237    */
 238   public static final short ACC_STATIC       = 0x0008;
 239 
 240   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 241    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 242    */
 243   public static final short ACC_FINAL        = 0x0010;
 244 
 245   /** One of the access flags for the Module attribute.
 246    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 247    */
 248   public static final short ACC_OPEN         = 0x0020;
 249

 251    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 256    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 266    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 268   public static final short ACC_BRIDGE       = 0x0040;
 269

 271    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 273   public static final short ACC_STATIC_PHASE = 0x0040;

 275   /** One of the access flags for fields.
 276    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 278   public static final short ACC_VOLATILE     = 0x0040;
 279 
 280   /** One of the access flags for fields.
 281    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 283   public static final short ACC_TRANSIENT    = 0x0080;
 284 
 285   /** One of the access flags for methods.
 286    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 287    */
 288   public static final short ACC_VARARGS      = 0x0080;

 290   /** One of the access flags for methods.
 291    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 293   public static final short ACC_NATIVE       = 0x0100;

 295   /** One of the access flags for classes.
 296    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 298   public static final short ACC_INTERFACE    = 0x0200;
 299 
 300   /** One of the access flags for methods or classes.
 301    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 303   public static final short ACC_ABSTRACT     = 0x0400;

 308   public static final short ACC_STRICT       = 0x0800;

 310   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, classes, MethodParameter attribute, or Module attribute.
 311    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 312    */
 313   public static final short ACC_SYNTHETIC    = 0x1000;
 314 
 315   /** One of the access flags for classes.
 316    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 317    */
 318   public static final short ACC_ANNOTATION   = 0x2000;

 320   /** One of the access flags for fields or classes.
 321    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 322    */
 323   public static final short ACC_ENUM         = 0x4000;

 325   // Applies to classes compiled by new compilers only
 326   /** One of the access flags for MethodParameter or Module attributes.
 327    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 328    */
 329   public static final short ACC_MANDATED     = (short) 0x8000;

 331   /** One of the access flags for classes.
 332    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC

 334   public static final short ACC_MODULE       = (short) 0x8000;

 336   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 337    *  @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 338    *  @deprecated Use {@link #MAX_ACC_FLAG_I}
 339    */
 340   @Deprecated
 341   public static final short MAX_ACC_FLAG     = ACC_ENUM;
 342 
 343   /** One of the access flags for fields, methods, or classes.
 344    * ACC_MODULE is negative as a short.
 345    * @see #ACC_PUBLIC
 346    * @since 6.4.0
 347    */
 348   public static final int MAX_ACC_FLAG_I = 0x8000; // ACC_MODULE is negative as a short
 349 
 350   // Note that do to overloading:
 351   // 'synchronized' is for methods, might be 'open' (if Module), 'super' (if class), or 'transitive' (if Module).
 352   // 'volatile'     is for fields,  might be 'bridge' (if method) or 'static_phase' (if Module)
 353   // 'transient'    is for fields,  might be 'varargs' (if method)
 354   // 'module'       is for classes, might be 'mandated' (if Module or MethodParameters)
 355   /**
 356    * The names of the access flags.
 357    */
 358   private static final String[] ACCESS_NAMES = {
 359     "public", "private", "protected", "static", "final", "synchronized",
 360     "volatile", "transient", "native", "interface", "abstract", "strictfp",
 361     "synthetic", "annotation", "enum", "module"
 362   };
 363 
 364   /** @since 6.0 */
 365   public static final int ACCESS_NAMES_LENGTH = ACCESS_NAMES.length;
 366 
 367   /**
 368    * @param index
 369    * @return the ACCESS_NAMES entry at the given index
 370    * @since 6.0
 371    */
 372   public static String getAccessName(final int index) {
 373       return ACCESS_NAMES[index];
 374   }

 393    */
 394   public static final byte CONSTANT_Integer            = 3;

 401   public static final byte CONSTANT_Float              = 4;

 546   /**
 547    * Maximum Constant Pool entries.
 548    * One of the limitations of the Java Virtual Machine.
 549    * @see <a href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.11-100-A">
 550    * The Java Virtual Machine Specification, Java SE 8 Edition, page 330, chapter 4.11.</a>
 551    */
 552   public static final int MAX_CP_ENTRIES     = 65535;
 553 
 554   /**
 555    * Maximum code size (plus one; the code size must be LESS than this)
 556    * One of the limitations of the Java Virtual Machine.
 557    * Note vmspec2 page 152 ("Limitations") says:
 558    * "The amount of code per non-native, non-abstract method is limited to 65536 bytes by
 559    * the sizes of the indices in the exception_table of the Code attribute (4.7.3),
 560    * in the LineNumberTable attribute (4.7.8), and in the LocalVariableTable attribute (4.7.9)."
 561    * However this should be taken as an upper limit rather than the defined maximum.
 562    * On page 134 (4.8.1 Static Constants) of the same spec, it says:
 563    * "The value of the code_length item must be less than 65536."
 564    * The entry in the Limitations section has been removed from later versions of the spec;
 565    * it is not present in the Java SE 8 edition.
 566    *
 567    * @see <a href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.7.3-300-E">
 568    * The Java Virtual Machine Specification, Java SE 8 Edition, page 104, chapter 4.7.3</a>
 569    */
 570   public static final int MAX_CODE_SIZE      = 65536; //bytes
 571 
 572   /**
 573    * The maximum number of dimensions in an array ({@value}).
 574    * One of the limitations of the Java Virtual Machine.
 575    *
 576    * @see <a href="http://docs.oracle.com/javase/specs/jvms/se8/html/jvms-4.html#jvms-4.3.2-150">
 577    * Field Descriptors in The Java Virtual Machine Specification</a>
 578    */
 579   public static final int MAX_ARRAY_DIMENSIONS = 255;
